When a new HTTP stream arrives (newStream() in ConnectionManagerImpl), it creates an ActiveStream\\n2. ActiveStream's FilterManager calls createFilterChain() which invokes the FilterChainFactory\\n3. APIs\\n\\n**envoy/http/filter_factory.h**: Defines the core filter factory types:\\n- `FilterFactoryCb`: Function callback used to wrap filter creation for new streams\\n- `FilterContext`: Contextual information (config_name, filter_name) passed to filter factories\\n- `FilterChainOptions`: Options for customizing filter chain creation\\n- `FilterChainManager`: Interface for applying filter factory callbacks to create filters\\n- `FilterChainFactory`: Main factory interface called when new HTTP streams are created\\n\\n**envoy/http/filter.h**: Defines core filter interfaces:\\n- `StreamFilterBase`: Base class with lifecycle methods (onDestroy, onStreamComplete, onLocalReply)\\n- `StreamDecoderFilter`: Interface for decoding filters with methods like decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), decodeTrailers()\\n- `StreamEncoderFilter`: Interface for encoding filters with methods like encodeHeaders(), encodeData(), encodeTrailers()\\n- `StreamFilter`: Combines both decoder and encoder interfaces\\n- `StreamFilterCallbacks`: Interface for filters to interact with the stream\\n- `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks`: Callbacks used to register filters (addStreamDecoderFilter, addStreamEncoderFilter, addStreamFilter)\\n\\n**envoy/server/filter_config.h**: Defines factory registry interfaces:\\n- `HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase`: Base class for HTTP filter factories\\n- `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`: Registered factories for named HTTP filters\\n- `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory`: Factories for upstream HTTP filters\\n\\n## Filter Manager & Per-Request Execution\\n\\n**source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc**: Core filter chain execution engine:\\n- `FilterManager`: Base class managing filter chain execution for a stream\\n- `DownstreamFilterManager`: Manages downstream (request) filter chains\\n- `ActiveStreamFilterBase`: Wraps decoder/encoder filters with iteration state\\n- `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl`: Implementation of FilterChainFactoryCallbacks that registers filters\\n- Key methods: `createFilterChain()` initializes the filter chain, `decodeHeaders()` iterates through decoder filters, `encodeHeaders()` iterates through encoder filters\\n- Per-filter state management and continuation logic\\n\\n**source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h/cc**: HTTP connection manager:\\n- `ConnectionManagerImpl`: Network filter that manages HTTP connections and creates streams\\n- `ActiveStream`: Represents a single HTTP stream with its filter manager\\n- Integrates with FilterManager to create and execute filter chains for new streams\\n\\n## Filter Factory Registry & Configuration\\n\\n**source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h/cc**: Filter factory processing:\\n- `FilterChainUtility`: Processes filter factory configurations and creates filter chains\\n- `FilterChainHelper`: Template class for processing filters from configuration\\n- `createFilterChainForFactories()`: Main function that applies filter factories to create filter instances\\n- Handles dynamic filter configuration via ECDS (Extension Config Discovery Service)\\n\\n**source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h**: Base classes for filter factories:\\n- `CommonFactoryBase`: Common implementation for all HTTP filter factories\\n- `FactoryBase`: Template base for standard HTTP filter factories\\n- `ExceptionFreeFactoryBase`: For factories that return Status instead of throwing exceptions\\n- `DualFactoryBase`: For filters that work in both downstream and upstream contexts\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n**source/common/http/filter_manager.h**: Filter iteration state management:\\n- Tracks iteration state (Continue, StopIteration, StopIterationAndBuffer, etc.)\\n- Manages buffering of headers, data, and trailers during filter execution\\n- Handles continuation callbacks when filters want to resume iteration\\n\\n**source/common/http/dependency_manager.h**: Validates filter chain dependencies:\\n- Ensures filters declare their dependencies correctly\\n- Validates that decode dependencies are satisfied by previous filters\\n\\n**source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h**: Configuration interfaces:\\n- Provides FilterChainFactory reference to connection manager\\n- Configuration for HTTP connection manager behavior\\n\\n**source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h**: Dynamic filter configuration:\\n- Supports ECDS for dynamic filter configuration updates\\n- Allows filters to be added/modified at runtime via xDS\\n\\n## Filter Chain Execution Flow\\n\\n1. When a new HTTP stream arrives (newStream() in ConnectionManagerImpl), it creates an ActiveStream\\n2. ActiveStream's FilterManager calls createFilterChain() which invokes the FilterChainFactory\\n3. FilterChainFactory calls createFilterChainForFactories() which applies each registered factory\\n4. Each factory returns a FilterFactoryCb that creates the actual filter instance\\n5. Filters are registered via FilterChainFactoryCallbacks (addStreamDecoderFilter, addStreamEncoderFilter)\\n6. For each request, the FilterManager iterates through decoder filters (decodeHeaders -> decodeData -> decodeTrailers)\\n7. For each response, the FilterManager iterates through encoder filters (encodeHeaders -> encodeData -> encodeTrailers)\\n8. Filter return codes (FilterHeadersStatus, FilterDataStatus, etc.) control iteration continuation\\n9. Filters can stop iteration, buffer data, or inject data back to the filter chain\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
